      206  export function isLeapYear(year: number): boolean {
      207    return year % 4 === 0 && (year % 100 !== 0 || year % 400 ===
            0);
      208  }
      209 +                                                              
      210 +/**                                                           
      211 + * Inverse of getWeekKey: the date nearest `nearISO` whose wee
          +k key matches ‚ÄĒ                                               
      212 + * lets a Tempora reference ("Tempora/Pent05-3") open on its r
          +eal calendar day.                                             
      213 + * Searches outward ¬Ī450 days (covers any movable-feast drift)
          +; null if the                                                 
      214 + * key never occurs (malformed).                              
      215 + */                                                           
      216 +export function dateForWeekKey(weekKey: string, nearISO: strin
          +g): string | null {                                           
      217 +  const near = parseISODate(nearISO);                         
      218 +  for (let off = 0; off <= 450; off++) {                      
      219 +    for (const sign of off === 0 ? [1] : [1, -1]) {           
      220 +      const d = new Date(near.getTime() + sign * off * 8640000
          +0);                                                           
      221 +      if (getWeekKey(d) === weekKey) return toISODate(d);     
      222 +    }                                                         
      223 +  }                                                           
      224 +  return null;                                                
      225 +}

      58 + * carries Office texts but no Mass sections says the preceding
         + Sunday's Mass                                                 
      59 + * ("de Dominica praecedenti", Divinum Officium behavior). Ever
         +y returned row                                                 
      60 + * keeps its real sourcePath, so delegated texts are labelled h
         +onestly.

      62 +export function massTextsForDay(db: CorpusDb, day: DayInfo): { 
         +texts: SectionText[]; sourcePath: string } {                   
      63 +  const primary = day.winner?.key ?? day.temporaPath;          
      64 +  let texts = db.getMassTexts(primary);                        
      65 +  if (texts.length > 0) return { texts, sourcePath: primary }; 
      66 +  const feria = primary.match(/^(Tempora\/.+)-[1-6]$/);        
      67 +  if (feria) {                                                 
      68 +    const sunday = `${feria[1]}-0`;                            
      69 +    texts = db.getMassTexts(sunday);                           
      70 +    if (texts.length > 0) return { texts, sourcePath: sunday };
      71 +  }                                                            
      72 +  return { texts: [], sourcePath: primary };                   
      73 +}

  deep-red Faithful segment, propers as interchange rings in the day's
  liturgical color, dashed rings for conditionals. Index-based

  synced to the reader via IntersectionObserver, seasonal chant switching (in
  Paschaltide the strip correctly shows the doubled Alleluia), and one-tap
  navigation to any section. Per your instruction it's suppressed where a view
  already shows its own map: the full-map view, and the office view on wide
  layouts where the side loop is visible.

  eight-hour cursus as a blue office-line strip, bidirectionally synced with the

      450  
      451 -### Build & Version Numbering                                 
      451 +### ‚õĒ Build & Version Numbering ‚ÄĒ COPY THE CANONICAL STAMPER,
          + NEVER RE-INVENT                                              
      452  
      453 -- Version name: **semantic** ‚ÄĒ `MAJOR.MINOR.PATCH[-qualifier]`
      454 -  - `MAJOR` ‚ÄĒ breaking change or major feature milestone      
      455 -  - `MINOR` ‚ÄĒ **auto-incremented by CI on every successful bui
          -ld** (see below)                                              
      456 -  - `PATCH` ‚ÄĒ bug fix or non-functional change; reset to 0 on 
          -MINOR bump                                                    
      457 -  - Qualifier: `alpha`, `beta`, `rc1`, etc. for pre-release   
      453 +**The canonical stamper lives at `~/Admin-Manual/versioning/up
          +date-version.sh`**                                            
      454 +(SOP: `~/Admin-Manual/versioning/README.md`; Node port:       
      455 +`~/CascadeProjects/StAndroidsMissal/scripts/stamp-version.mjs`
          +; bash lineage:                                               
      456 +Kintsugi-Unbroken `tauri2/scripts/update-version.sh`). Startin
          +g any project's                                               
      457 +versioning from scratch is a **violation** ‚ÄĒ copy the script, 
          +fill in the three                                             
      458 +`PRODUCT_*` vars, wire it into the build. Every project that r
          +e-derived this                                                
      459 +logic shipped the same defect and burned a session on it.     
      460  
      459 -- **Auto-increment rule**: every successful CI build bumps `MI
          -NOR` and resets `PATCH`                                       
      460 -  to `0`. The CI pipeline is the only thing that writes versio
          -n numbers ‚ÄĒ never                                             
      461 -  hand-edit them mid-cycle. MINOR is the heartbeat of the proj
          -ect.                                                          
      461 +- **THE invariant re-inventions keep losing: the bump lives IN
          +SIDE the stamper.**                                           
      462 +  `MINOR` increments **unconditionally on every stamper invoca
          +tion**. A stamper                                             
      463 +  that only *reads* a version file produces `v1.0.<build>` for
          +ever ‚ÄĒ the                                                    
      464 +  "impossible pattern". If the script has no `MINOR=$((MINOR +
          + 1))` line, it is                                             
      465 +  broken by construction.                                     
      466  
      463 -- **Cross-platform parity**: all platform manifests must carry
          - the same version string                                      
      464 -  at any given commit. The single source of truth is a top-lev
          -el `version.txt` (or                                          
      465 -  equivalent root-level version file); each platform's build s
          -cript reads from it:                                          
      466 -  - Android: `versionName` in `build.gradle.kts` via `readVers
          -ionFile()`                                                    
      467 -  - iOS/macOS: `MARKETING_VERSION` in `project.pbxproj` via `a
          -gvtool` or xcconfig                                           
      468 -  - Web/Node: `version` in `package.json` via `npm version` sc
          -ripted from the same file                                     
      469 -  - Desktop (Tauri): `version` in `tauri.conf.json`           
      470 -  Never let platforms drift. A release with mismatched version
          - strings is a build                                           
      471 -  failure.                                                    
      467 +- Scheme: `MAJOR.MINOR.BUILD`                                 
      468 +  - `MAJOR` ‚ÄĒ manual milestone (hand-edit `version.txt`, once 
          +per milestone;                                                
      469 +    MINOR resets to 0)                                        
      470 +  - `MINOR` ‚ÄĒ the heartbeat: auto-bumped by the stamper on **e
          +very build**                                                  
      471 +    (CI or local ‚ÄĒ whoever builds, bumps)                     
      472 +  - `BUILD` ‚ÄĒ epoch-minutes % 100000, 5-digit zero-padded, dis
          +play-only                                                     
      473 +- `versionCode = MAJOR * 100000 + MINOR` (BUILD excluded ‚ÄĒ Pla
          +y needs monotonic);                                           
      474 +  never hand-edited.                                          
      475 +- **Cross-platform parity**: `version.txt` (single line) is th
          +e sole source of                                              
      476 +  truth; `version.json` is the runtime mirror (version, versio
          +nCode, buildDate,                                             
      477 +  productName, packageName); package.json / tauri.conf.json / 
          +Cargo.toml /                                                  
      478 +  gen/android/tauri.properties / pbxproj are stamped outputs. 
          +Mismatched                                                    
      479 +  strings at a commit = build failure.                        
      480 +- `release.lock` freezes values across a multi-artifact releas
          +e; delete it to                                               
      481 +  resume bumping.                                             
      482 +- **Identifier hygiene**: `packageName` in version.json must e
          +qual the Tauri                                                
      483 +  `identifier`/`applicationId` exactly ‚ÄĒ no underscores (iOS r
          +ejects), no                                                   
      484 +  hyphens (Tauri rejects). On rename, grep the stamper's hered
          +oc too.                                                       
      485  
      473 -- Android `versionCode`: computed from version, never hand-edi
          -ted:                                                          
      474 -  ```                                                         
      475 -  versionCode = MAJOR * 10_000 + MINOR * 100 + PATCH          
      476 -  ```                                                         
      477 -  e.g. `1.3.7` ‚Üí `10307`. Monotonically increasing; Play Store
          - rejects regressions.                                         
      486 +### ‚õĒ Mandatory App Chrome ‚ÄĒ Splash, About, visible version (
          +all GUI apps)                                                 
      487  
      479 -- Build number: `git rev-list --count HEAD`, appended as build
          - metadata: `1.3.0+42`.                                        
      488 +Universal, non-negotiable, in scope from the FIRST build ‚ÄĒ ret
          +rofitting loses a                                             
      489 +session every time:                                           
      490  
      491 +1. **Splash screen** on launch: product name, logo/mark, full 
          +version string                                                
      492 +   (`MAJOR.MINOR.BUILD`), copyright `Robin L. M. Cheung, MBA`.
      493 +2. **Help | About** menu/dialog: product name, full version + 
          +versionCode,                                                  
      494 +   build date (from `version.json`), copyright, license line. 
      495 +3. **Version bottom-right on artifacts**: every shipped UI sur
          +face (main                                                    
      496 +   window/page footer) renders the version string bottom-right
          +, small and                                                   
      497 +   unobtrusive, sourced from `version.json` at runtime ‚ÄĒ never
          + hardcoded.                                                   
      498 +   Screenshots/exports/PDF artifacts inherit it so any artifac
          +t is traceable                                                
      499 +   to its build.                                              
      500 +                                                              
      501  ### Reference Build Workflow

‚óŹ Everything is landed and pushed. Full wrap-up of this turn:

  1. Your original question: how does Divinum Officium render missing portions?

  From the vendored engine itself
  (VENDORED/divinum-officium/web/cgi-bin/DivinumOfficium/SetupString.pl):

  Language layering ‚ÄĒ missing translations show Latin, never blanks. Every
  non-Latin file is parsed as a layer over its fallback: English layers on
  Latin; other languages layer on the fallback language, recursively
  (dash-variants like Deutsch-Koeln strip to Deutsch). The merge is one line ‚ÄĒ
  ${$new_sections}{$_} ||= ${$base_sections}{$_} under the comment "Fill in the
  missing things from the layer below" (SetupString.pl:622-624). So when an
  English file lacks GradualeP, DO renders the Latin text in the English column.
  No generation, no gap.

  File-level fallback works the same way: checkfile (SetupString.pl:785-820)
  tries the requested language's file ‚Üí fallback language's file ‚Üí Latin's file.

  Hard failure marker. Only when even Latin lacks a referenced section does DO
  emit a literal inline string: "$ftitle:$section is missing!"
  (SetupString.pl:539) ‚ÄĒ visible in the output, never silent.

  Implication for us: our reader currently renders "‚ÄĒ" for a NULL English
  column, which is worse than upstream behavior. The cheap, faithful interim
  (until OA.5's S‚ÜíA‚ÜíC routes supply real translations) is DO's move: render the
  Latin in the English pane flagged latine tantum. Say the word and I'll wire it
  ‚ÄĒ it's a small change in the bilingual pane renderer.

  2. Architecture docs ‚ÄĒ now genuinely current

  You caught a real gap: my session's contract had gone into the superseded v1
  doc. Now consolidated into the authoritative DOCS/ARCHITECTURE.md: Decision 17
  (ever-present map, flyouts, ferial delegation), two new data-flow paragraphs
  (reader path amended; map-strip position sync), and ¬ß8 rows for every new
  entity (MapStrip, MapFlyout, stripStations, stationForAnchor, stationIncipits,
  STATION_INFO/HOUR_INFO, massTextsForDay, dateForWeekKey) plus corrected
  shipped rows (App/SubwayMap/ReaderView/OfficeView/MeaningPanel/computus/tests
  44). The v1 doc now carries only a pointer, and CHECKLIST Phase M cites the
  authoritative doc.

  3. Mid-turn fixes, all verified live

  - Media slot removed from the flyout ‚ÄĒ you're right, it violated "no
  placeholder data" and would have shipped. The 39-asset production briefs stay
  in stationLore.ts + DOCS/MEDIA-PLAN.md (docs, not UI); the flyout gains a
  media renderer only when real assets exist.
  - Concept tags are now accordions with evidence: "‚Ėł Hymn ¬∑ 790 instances"
  expands to the actual linked instances (humanized SimilarHitRows,
  click-through to source day, top 20 shown) ‚ÄĒ no more "trust me bro."
  Auto-clusters get a small auto badge with the ugly Auto: ‚Ä¶_ prefix cleaned.
  - Mandatory app chrome shipped here: splash (product + version + copyright on
  the corpus-loading screen), Help ¬∑ About rail entry with full
  version/versionCode/build date/provenance, and v1.2.30403 bottom-right on
  every surface, all read from version.json at runtime. Tests 44/44, tsc clean.

  4. Versioning ‚ÄĒ root cause, fix, and why it kept happening

  This repo: stamp-version.mjs only read version.json; nothing ever bumped minor
  ‚Üí 1.0.<epoch-minutes> forever. Rewritten as a Node port of the working
  Kintsugi tauri2 script: MINOR bumps unconditionally inside the stamper,
  version.txt canonical, version.json runtime mirror, versionCode = MAJOR*100000
  + MINOR, release.lock freeze. Verified: two runs produced 1.1.30403 ‚Üí
  1.2.30403, versionCode 100001 ‚Üí 100002, all five manifests in lockstep.

  The Kintsugi underscore: you did change it ‚ÄĒ tauri2/tauri.conf.json says
  kintsugitarot and the tauri2 script agrees; only the root-level v1 script
  still wrote kintsugi_tarot, and per your note v1 stays live until the tauri2
  web app deploys at kintsugi.robin.mba ‚ÄĒ so I fixed that one line in place.

  Why every single project: the answer turned out to be structural. The
  compressed-spine rules regime on your Forgejo claude-global-rules repo already
  codifies this entire versioning convention (BUILD_CONVENTIONS.md, down to
  "Conditional MINOR bumps ‚ÄĒ banned") ‚ÄĒ but msi4090 had no ~/.claude git tree at
  all, so every project born on this machine never saw it. I bootstrapped this
  host into the sync:

  - ~/.claude is now a working tree on main = the spine regime (which is also
  what this message's system context now reflects).
  - The old long-form CLAUDE.md (including my earlier edits) is preserved on
  pushed branch msi4090-local-20260711 ‚ÄĒ nothing lost, merge/discard at your
  leisure: https://git.robin.mba/rcheung/claude-global-rules/compare/main...msi4
  090-local-20260711
  - Pushed to main: BUILD_CONVENTIONS.md now carries ready-to-copy pointers
  (~/Admin-Manual/versioning/, the Node port here, Kintsugi tauri2 lineage) + a
  new Mandatory App Chrome section (splash / About / version bottom-right) ‚ÄĒ so
  both SOPs reach every synced host.
  - Pushed to Admin-Manual (GitHub): versioning/update-version.sh template +
  README, explicitly subordinated to BUILD_CONVENTIONS.md so there's one truth.
  (I left your other uncommitted Admin-Manual changes and the credentials PNG
  untouched.)

  One decision is yours: whether to merge or discard the parked
  msi4090-local-20260711 branch ‚ÄĒ its unique content (stamper + chrome SOPs) has
  already been re-landed into the spine's proper files, so it's now purely the
  historical long-form regime.

  2. The sync task fails instantly server-side without updating the timestamp ‚ÄĒ

  surfaces the actual error message that the API hides.
  3. Outbound network from the v15 container to github.com (it needs to pull
  ~180MB; if egress or DNS in the container is broken, syncs die immediately).
